Descendants of Hiram (Carter) Pipes

Generation One

1. Hiram (Carter)1 Pipes was born circa 1784 in Surry Co., North Carolina. He married Elizabeth Allison.

Elizabeth Allison was born on 28 July 1792.

The 10 known children of Hiram (Carter)1 Pipes and Elizabeth Allison were as follows:

  • + 2. i. Ama Elvira2 Pipes, born circa 1817; married William Leander (Grassy Jim) Robbins.

  • + 3. ii. Thomas Pipes, born 1819; married Julia Barlow; married Elizabeth Winkler.

  • 4. iii. Sarah Pipes was born in 1822. She died before 1900.

  • + 5. iv. Rachel Pipes, born 23 August 1823; married William Lewis.

  • + 6. v. Rebecca Pipes, born 23 August 1823; married Samuel Day.

  • + 7. vi. Larkin Pipes, born 16 October 1825; married Elizabeth Lewis.

  • + 8. vii. William Riley Pipes, born 5 March 1828; married Emily Penley.

  • + 9. viii. John Wiley Pipes, born 5 March 1828; married Violet Matilda Brown.

  • + 10. ix. Susanna Pipes, born 13 April 1830; married John Day.

  • + 11. x. Jesse Pipes, born 31 December 1832; married Julia Triplett.

He died in Kinston, North Carolina during the Civil War as a Confederate soldier.
